General Public: Output (a) is the correct implementation of the Boyer-Moore Voting Algorithm, which is designed to find the majority element in an array. This algorithm works by iterating through the array and keeping a count of the current candidate for the majority element. If the count becomes zero, it updates the candidate to the current number. The count is incremented if the current number is equal to the candidate, otherwise, it is decremented. This approach ensures that the candidate with the highest frequency will be returned. This can be useful when the order of the common elements is important or when further processing of the entire list is required.
